***согрешить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:согрешить.html>согреши́ть</a> (23334)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:согрешить.html>согреши́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sogrešítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грешить.html>греши́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sin <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to commit a sin</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">соде́йство</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sodéjstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***содержать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:содержать.html>содержа́ть</a> (2534)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:содержать.html>содержа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">soderžátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>no perfective form</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>to contain, to hold
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вещество.html>вещество́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:содержать.html>соде́ржит</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:натрий.html>на́трий</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto veščestvó <b>sodéržit</b> nátrij.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This substance <b>contains</b> sodium.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to maintain, to keep (in a certain state)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:содержать.html>содержа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чистота.html>чистоте́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>soderžátʹ</b> v čistoté</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to keep clean</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to support, to keep, to provide with all necessities</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:содержаться.html>содержа́ться</a> (4555)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:содержать.html>содержа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">soderžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:содержаться.html>содержа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">soderžátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to contain, to hold
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́той</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́ге</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:содержаться.html>соде́ржится</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полезный.html>поле́зных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сведение.html>све́дений</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V étoj kníge <b>sodéržitsja</b> mnógo poléznyx svédenij.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">This book contains a lot of useful information.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:содержать.html>содержа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">soderžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***содрать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:содрать.html>содра́ть</a> (9133)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>со-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">so-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драть.html>драть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dratʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:содрать.html>содра́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sodrátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драть.html>драть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдирать.html>сдира́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to strip, to strip off, to scratch off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:содрать.html>содра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кожа.html>ко́жу</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sodrátʹ</b> kóžu (s)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to skin; strip the skin off</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:содрать.html>содра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кора.html>кору́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> берёзы</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sodrátʹ</b> korú s berjózy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bark a birch</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:содрать.html>содра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шкура.html>шку́ру</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:животный.html>живо́тного</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sodrátʹ</b> škúru s živótnovo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to flay/skin an animal</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to charge
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:содрать.html>содра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:бешеный.html>бе́шеную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цена.html>це́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sodrátʹ</b> s kovó-libo béšenuju cénu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to rip someone off; charge someone an exorbitant price</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to copy, to crib, to plagiarize</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>со-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">so-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрогнуть.html>дро́гнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">drógnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:содрогнуться.html>содрогну́ться</a> (11527)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:содрогаться.html>содрога́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sodrogátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:содрогнуться.html>содрогну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sodrognútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:содрогаться.html>содрога́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to shudder</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соединить.html>соедини́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sojedinítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соединение.html>соедине́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sojedinénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соединение.html>соедине́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соединение.html>соедине́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соединение.html>соедине́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>joining, junction</li>
<li>connection</li>
<li>combination, union</li>
<li>joint, junction</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> compound</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> formation <i>(refers to a corps, a division, or a brigade; also informally, an army)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> combination</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:соединить.html>соедини́ть</a> (3018)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>со-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">so-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:единый.html>еди́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jedín</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соединить.html>соедини́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sojedinítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соединять.html>соединя́ть</a></b>)
</p>

<li>to connect, to put through</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to combine</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:соединиться.html>соедини́ться</a> (8845)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соединить.html>соедини́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sojedinítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соединиться.html>соедини́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sojedinítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соединяться.html>соединя́ться</a></b>)

<ol><li>to unite</li>
<li>to connect, to join</li>
<li>to get connected, to get linked, to connect</li>

<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соединить.html>соедини́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sojedinítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***соединяться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:соединяться.html>соединя́ться</a> (10473)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соединять.html>соединя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sojedinjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соединяться.html>соединя́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sojedinjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соединиться.html>соедини́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to unite</li>
<li>to connect, to join</li>
<li>to get connected, to get linked, to connect</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to combine</li>
